A variable\n// with a random value in it is stored onto the stack before the local variables\n// are allocated. Upon exiting the block, the stored value is checked. If it's\n// changed, then there was some sort of violation and the program aborts.\n//\n//===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//\n\n#ifndef LLVM_CODEGEN_STACKPROTECTOR_H\n#define LLVM_CODEGEN_STACKPROTECTOR_H\n\n#include \"llvm/Analysis/DomTreeUpdater.h\"\n#include \"llvm/CodeGen/MachineFrameInfo.h\"\n#include Module;\nclass TargetLoweringBase;\nclass TargetMachine;\n\nclass SSPLayoutInfo {\n  friend class StackProtectorPass;\n  friend class SSPLayoutAnalysis;\n  friend class StackProtector;\n  static constexpr unsigned DefaultSSPBufferSize = 8;\n\n  /// A mapping of AllocaInsts to their required SSP layout.\n  using SSPLayoutMap =\n      DenseMap<const AllocaInst *, MachineFrameInfo::SSPLayoutKind>;\n\n  /// Layout - Mapping of allocations to the required SSPLayoutKind.\n  /// StackProtector analysis will update this map when determining if an\n  /// AllocaInst triggers a stack protector.\n  SSPLayoutMap Layout;\n\n  /// The minimum size of buffers that will receive stack smashing\n  /// protection when -fstack-protection is used.\n  unsigned SSPBufferSize = DefaultSSPBufferSize;\n\n  bool RequireStackProtector = false;\n\n  // A prologue is generated.\n  bool HasPrologue = false;\n\n  // IR checking code is generated.\n  bool HasIRCheck = false;\n\npublic:\n  // Return true if StackProtector is supposed to be handled by SelectionDAG.\n  bool shouldEmitSDCheck(const BasicBlock &BB) const;\n\n  void copyToMachineFrameInfo(MachineFrameInfo &MFI) const;\n};\n\nclass SSPLayoutAnalysis : public AnalysisInfoMixin<SSPLayoutAnalysis> {\n  friend AnalysisInfoMixin<SSPLayoutAnalysis>;\n  using SSPLayoutMap = SSPLayoutInfo::SSPLayoutMap;\n\n  static AnalysisKey Key;\n\npublic:\n  using Result = SSPLayoutInfo;\n\n  Result run(Function &F, FunctionAnalysisManager &FAM);\n\n  /// Check whether or not \\p F needs a stack protector based upon the stack\n  /// protector level.\n  static bool requiresStackProtector(Function *F,\n                                     SSPLayoutMap *Layout = nullptr);\n};\n\nclass StackProtectorPass : public PassInfoMixin<StackProtectorPass> {\n  const TargetMachine *TM;\n\npublic:\n  explicit StackProtectorPass(const TargetMachine &TM) : TM(&TM) {}\n  PreservedAnalyses run(Function &F, FunctionAnalysisManager &FAM);\n};\n\nclass StackProtector : public FunctionPass {\nprivate:\n  /// A mapping of AllocaInsts to their required SSP layout.\n  using SSPLayoutMap = SSPLayoutInfo::SSPLayoutMap;\n\n  const TargetMachine *TM = nullptr;\n\n  Function *F = nullptr;\n  Module *M = nullptr;\n\n  std::optional<DomTreeUpdater> DTU;\n\n  SSPLayoutInfo LayoutInfo;\n\npublic:\n  static char ID; // Pass identification, replacement for typeid.\n\n  StackProtector();\n\n  SSPLayoutInfo &getLayoutInfo() { return LayoutInfo; }\n\n  void getAnalysisUsage(AnalysisUsage &AU) const override;\n\n  // Return true if StackProtector is supposed to be handled by SelectionDAG.\n  bool shouldEmitSDCheck(const BasicBlock &BB) const {\n    return LayoutInfo.shouldEmitSDCheck(BB);\n  }\n\n  bool runOnFunction(Function &Fn) override;\n\n  void copyToMachineFrameInfo(MachineFrameInfo &MFI) const {\n    LayoutInfo.copyToMachineFrameInfo(MFI);\n  }\n\n  /// Check whether or not \\p F needs a stack protector based upon the stack\n  /// protector level.\n  static bool requiresStackProtector(Function *F,\n                                     SSPLayoutMap *Layout = nullptr) {\n    return SSPLayoutAnalysis::requiresStackProtector(F, Layout);\n  }\n};\n\n} // end namespace llvm\n\n#endif // Class: StackProtectorPass (modern new-PM pass) and StackProtector (legacy pass)\\n   - Implements stack canary insertion at function prologue and epilogue\\n   - Inserts comparison checks that call __stack_chk_fail() if the canary has been overwritten\\n   - Key functions: InsertStackProtectors() inserts prologue/epilogue code, CreateFailBB() creates failure path\\n   - Uses SSPLayoutAnalysis to determine which allocas require protection based on buffer size\\n   - Supports multiple protection levels: -fstack-protector, -fstack-protector-strong, -fstack-protector-all\\n\\n2. **SafeStack Pass** (llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStack.cpp & Header: llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/SafeStack.h)\\n   - Primary Class: SafeStackPass (new-PM interface) and SafeStack (implementation class)\\n   - Separates stack into safe stack (LLVM-managed, accessed via memory-safe operations) and unsafe stack (runtime-allocated)\\n   - Protects against buffer overflows by isolating unsafe allocations to a separately managed stack\\n   - Key methods: getStackGuard() retrieves the stack canary, checkStackGuard() validates it at function exit\\n   - moveStaticAllocasToUnsafeStack() and moveDynamicAllocasToUnsafeStack() move risky allocations\\n   - IsSafeStackAlloca() determines whether allocations are safe based on access patterns\\n\\n3. **SafeStackLayout** frame allocations\\n   - Manages stack coloring and alignment requirements for the unsafe stack\\n   - Functions: addObject() registers allocations, computeLayout() calculates frame layout\\n\\n4. **Runtime Stack Check Implementation** (libc/src/compiler/__stack_chk_fail.h & libc/src/compiler/generic/__stack_chk_fail.cpp)\\n   - Function: __stack_chk_fail() - runtime function called when stack corruption is detected\\n   - Global: __stack_chk_guard - random canary value initialized at startup\\n   - Implementation prints \\\"stack smashing detected\\\" message and calls abort()\\n   - Part of LLVM's libc (not traditional compiler-rt), providing the C library runtime support\\n\\nThese components work together: StackProtector inserts canary checks that call __stack_chk_fail on corruption, while SafeStack provides an additional layer by segregating unsafe allocations to a separately managed stack region, with SafeStackLayout managing the efficient allocation of this unsafe
